<div id="review_2003446563" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2003446563" />
    <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583236251p2/3575839.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2003446563?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog">Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-romance">genre-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-thriller">genre-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=kiddie-winks">kiddie-winks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=best-of-the-best-2017">best-of-the-best-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2003446563" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3590057979194150261"><a href='http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2017/06/say-youre-sorry-by-melinda-leigh.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550694r/16122391.jpg%20' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I am still relatively new to the thriller genre, I like to dip my toe in every now and then, however, in this book Melinda Leigh has tempted me to belly flop right in. Say You’re Sorry captivated me from page one as you witness the murder first hand, after that, it wasn’t a want, it was a need; I needed to keep reading and find out the full story.<br/><br/>Morgan Dane is our main character, she’s been widowed for two years and has 3 adorable small children, who she parents with the help of her father.</span>
  <span id="freeText3590057979194150261" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2017/06/say-youre-sorry-by-melinda-leigh.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441550694r/16122391.jpg%20" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I am still relatively new to the thriller genre, I like to dip my toe in every now and then, however, in this book Melinda Leigh has tempted me to belly flop right in. Say You’re Sorry captivated me from page one as you witness the murder first hand, after that, it wasn’t a want, it was a need; I needed to keep reading and find out the full story.<br><br>Morgan Dane is our main character, she’s been widowed for two years and has 3 adorable small children, who she parents with the help of her father. Now, she has decided it’s time for her to go back to work as a prosecutor. But, just as she’s about to start her baby sitter is horrifically murdered and her neighbour is accused of the slaying. Morgan doesn’t buy it. So with the help of her private investigator and former high school boyfriend, she decides to take up his defence.<br><br>This book is so easy to get into, Morgan is such an identifiable figure, a single mother trying to do the best for her children and now juggling a stressful job. A stressful job where she isn’t sure she’s doing the right thing. And then there’s Lance the PI assisting her with the case and a guy with some pressures of his own. The murder case itself, although interesting to follow, as soon as the murderer popped up I figured it out correctly but that didn’t stop me from enjoying the ride to get there.<br><br>It was Morgan and her relationship with people, her blossoming romance with Lance, her devotion to her family, her dedication to helping Nick – the young man accused of murder – that kept me glued to the book. I can’t wait to read more in this series and I will definitely be looking up some more Melinda Leigh.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3590057979194150261" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <a title="Anna&#39;s Herding Cats" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna&#39;s Herding Cats" href="/user/show/5417092-anna-s-herding-cats">Anna&#39;s Herding Cats</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2497505115" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13233236512273623187">Well that was good. <br/><br/>The Gist: Morgan's babysitter has been brutally murdered. And the boy next door has been accused of the crime. Morgan, though, is certain he's not guilty and decides to defend him in court even if it's the unpopular opinion. Now she just has to prove he's innocent. <br/><br/>The Story:<br/><br/>I enjoyed the mystery. The storyline bops around for different points of view-- Morgan, the boy accused and the killer-- as the crime is investigated and days go by. It was a good mystery. Kept me interes</span>
  <span id="freeText13233236512273623187" style="display:none">Well that was good. <br /><br />The Gist: Morgan's babysitter has been brutally murdered. And the boy next door has been accused of the crime. Morgan, though, is certain he's not guilty and decides to defend him in court even if it's the unpopular opinion. Now she just has to prove he's innocent. <br /><br />The Story:<br /><br />I enjoyed the mystery. The storyline bops around for different points of view-- Morgan, the boy accused and the killer-- as the crime is investigated and days go by. It was a good mystery. Kept me interested and wondering how they'd piece it all together. There's a hint of romance between Morgan and her friend who is helping her. I liked them as a team and how they interacted. It'll be fun seeing how their relationship evolves now that she's back in town and they're coworkers. <br /><br />The Narration:<br /><br />This was my first time with Chris Dukehart. She took a little getting used to. Took me a bit to find the right speed. I ended up listening at 1.0x which is really slow for me but what suited her narration best. She did a good job with the male/female voices. My main quip with her was the children's voices (Morgan's kids). Not a deal breaker, though. But she did a good job with pacing and once I was used to her voice (couple chapters) it was easy to get lost in the narration and before I realized 11 hours had passed in less than 2 days. Whoa! I'll listen to the rest on audio without hesitation. </span>

<div id="review_3551778497" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3551778497" />
    <a title="Lauren" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4731410-lauren"><img alt="Lauren" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387526203p2/4731410.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3551778497?book_show_action=true">Oct 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lauren" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lauren" href="/user/show/4731410-lauren">Lauren</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4731410-lauren?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4731410-lauren?shelf=widows-weeds">widows-weeds</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3551778497" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17988876682381519241"><b>Say You're Sorry</b><br/>4 Stars<br/><br/><u>Series note:</u> This is book #1 in the spin-off from <i>Scarlet Falls</i>. While the thriller plot is standalone, the characters are introduced in the previous series, and their backstories are essential to the characterization. <br/><br/>An exciting romantic suspense with an appealing couple and some gripping scenes. Nevertheless, there are one or two issues that prevent this from being a 5 star read. <br/><br/>Morgan and Lance's slow-burn romance is sweet, and the fact that they want more from each o</span>
  <span id="freeText17988876682381519241" style="display:none"><b>Say You're Sorry</b><br />4 Stars<br /><br /><u>Series note:</u> This is book #1 in the spin-off from <i>Scarlet Falls</i>. While the thriller plot is standalone, the characters are introduced in the previous series, and their backstories are essential to the characterization. <br /><br />An exciting romantic suspense with an appealing couple and some gripping scenes. Nevertheless, there are one or two issues that prevent this from being a 5 star read. <br /><br />Morgan and Lance's slow-burn romance is sweet, and the fact that they want more from each other than to simply scratch an itch adds to their emotional connection. They each have their own issues to overcome, and it will be interesting to see how this plays out in later books. <br /><br />The suspense plot is well-paced with several action-packed moments. Nevertheless, some plot points lack sufficient development - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Nick's blood aversion, the hit on him in prison, and who saved his life <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, and there are also inconsistencies in the killer's POV. As such, it is difficult for the reader to pin down his identity, and the revelation comes out of the blue.<br /><br />This is a somewhat nitpicky observation, but I also found the language used to be jarring at times, particularly phrases related to the romance, i.e., <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[girl parts, swelling ovaries, superior genes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />In sum, <b>Say You're Sorry</b> is the beginning of a promising storyline with compelling primary and secondary characters. I look forward to continuing with the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17988876682381519241" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Ea/yVcWpQARVnIpZR/tNzHA/GHdAu2uCGZ4nX5xsT9QriZuHfveJbPK3PjiwDkcTpmD/v4425eVC4GHuUS+9Tg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('p3LRMGcWShPFaKKeTGY1qQLAjzYzafDzq82i8+gzQcmdVLji3EiDe2JDFv+7kz921J9o/v3kfpTws+RCJXCzUw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer6403074251858614955">#1 Wall Street Journal and #1 Amazon bestselling author Melinda Leigh is a fully recovered banker who learned that writing books is way more fun than analyzing financial statements. Melinda’s debut novel, SHE CAN RUN, was nominated for Best First Novel by the International Thriller Writers.   <span id="freeText6403074251858614955" style="display:none">#1 Wall Street Journal and #1 Amazon bestselling author Melinda Leigh is a fully recovered banker who learned that writing books is way more fun than analyzing financial statements. Melinda’s debut novel, SHE CAN RUN, was nominated for Best First Novel by the International Thriller Writers. Since then, she has garnered numerous writing accolades, including two RITA® Award nominations and an induction into the NJ Romance Writers Hall of Fame. Her novels have sold more than 7.5 million copies across the world. Melinda loves martial arts, rescue dogs, and sea turtles. <br /><br /><b>WEBSITE: </b><a href="https://www.melindaeigh.com" rel="nofollow noopener">https://www.melindaleigh.com/</a><br /><br /><b>FACEBOOK: </b><a href="https://www.facebook.com/melindaleighauthorpage/" rel="nofollow noopener">https://www.facebook.com/melindaleighauthorpage/</a><br /><br /><b>TWITTER: </b><a href="https://twitter.com/MelindaLeigh1" rel="nofollow noopener">https://twitter.com/MelindaLeigh1</a></span>
